[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview and Root Cause:[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The SSRF arises when parsing “extended properties” XML inside XSSF [0m[1;39m([0m[39m.xlsx[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXSSFB [0m[1;39m([0m[39m.xlsb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m extractors: both call [0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout disabling external entities or DTDs, so a malicious file can embed external[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentity references that trigger outbound HTTP/socket connections.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Core Strategy:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Replace all direct calls to [0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m in [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mgetExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m methods of:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • org.apache.poi.xssf.extractor.XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor  [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     • org.apache.poi.xssf.extractor.XSSFBEventBasedExcelExtractor  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     with calls to the centrally hardened factory provided by [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35morg.apache.poi.util.XMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, which by default disables DTD [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mloading and external entity resolution.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This change reuses existing secure configuration in XMLHelper, preserving all [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcurrent XML parsing behavior [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnamespace-awareness, non-validating[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m while blocking [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted external accesses.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Detailed Patch Steps:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.getExtendedProps [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mpoi-ooxml/[0m[33m...[0m[35m/[0m[95mXSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.java[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Locate:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          try [0m[1;39m([0m[39mInputStream is = [0m[1;35mpart.getInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              SAXParser parser = [0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m              [0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, new [0m[1;35mExtendedPropertiesHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtext[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Change to:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          SAXParser parser = [0m[1;35mXMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          [0m[1;35mparser.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[39mis, new [0m[1;35mExtendedPropertiesHandler[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtext[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Ensure the import for XMLHelper [0m[1;39m([0m[39morg.apache.poi.util.XMLHelper[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is present.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRemove or ignore the old import for SAXParserFactory if unused elsewhere.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. XSSFBEventBasedExcelExtractor.getExtendedProps [0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mpoi-ooxml/[0m[33m...[0m[35m/[0m[95mXSSFBEventBasedExcelExtractor.java[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m      - Apply the identical replacement in its extended-properties parsing method:[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m          replace [0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m with [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mXMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Functionality:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - [0m[1;35mXMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m sets:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       • [0m[1;35mfactory.setValidating[0m[1;39m([0m[39mfalse[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       • [0m[1;35mfactory.setNamespaceAware[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtrue[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       • FEATURE_SECURE_PROCESSING = true;  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       • FEATURE_LOAD_DTD_GRAMMAR = false;  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       • FEATURE_LOAD_EXTERNAL_DTD = false;  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       • FEATURE_EXTERNAL_ENTITIES = false;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This matches existing parser behavior except for tightening security. All [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhandlers [0m[1;39m([0m[39mExtendedPropertiesHandler[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and input streams remain unchanged.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Justification:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Centralizing secure parser configuration ensures consistent hardening across [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mall XML parsing entry points.[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Avoids code duplication of security features and leverages an already-tested [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mutility [0m[1;39m([0m[39mXMLHelper[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Eliminates attacker-controlled external entity resolution, fully mitigating [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe SSRF vector reported by Jazzer.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Side Effects and Mitigation:[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Disallowing DTDs and external entities may break parsing of legitimately [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDTD-dependent extended-properties documents. However, Excel OOXML [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextended-properties XML never relies on external DTDs; it uses simple elements and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattributes only. Existing Apache POI tests for extended-properties parsing will [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcontinue to pass.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No changes to public APIs or fuzzer harness code are required. Fuzzer will [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstill traverse getExtendedProps, but without being able to resolve external URIs.[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. References and Similar Patterns:[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Other parts of Apache POI [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., core POIXMLProperties handlers[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m already [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreference [0m[1;35mXMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m for secure XML parsing.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Aligns with upstream POI hardening guidelines for secure XML processing.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m. Validation:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run existing POI unit tests [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpoi-ooxml and poi modules[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; all should pass [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithout changes.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Re-run Jazzer fuzz harness to confirm the SSRF sanitizer is no longer [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggered on extended-properties XML.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXSSF extractor tried to fetch external XML resources during Excel extraction. The [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproposed patch edits `XSSFBEventBasedExcelExtractor.java` by removing the [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`java.io.IOException` import and adding two new imports [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`EXTENDED_PROPERTIES` and [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`XMLHelper`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, presumably to switch to a secure XML helper API. After applying the [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatch, the overall build succeeds in most modules, but the `poi-ooxml` module fails[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto compile. The compiler reports “cannot find symbol: class IOException” in [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`XSSFBEventBasedExcelExtractor.java`, leading to a build failure.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.getExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Stack trace shows an attempt to open an HTTP connection to `jazze.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m[39m` while [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolving XML entities via Java’s standard `HttpURLConnection`.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This indicates that external entity processing or schema resolution in POI’s [0m     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview and Root Cause  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The compilation errors stem solely from removing the `java.io.IOException` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimport in `XSSFBEventBasedExcelExtractor.java`. Restoring this import resolves the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“cannot find symbol: IOException” build failures.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The SSRF vulnerability arises because both the XLSX [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and XLSB [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`XSSFBEventBasedExcelExtractor`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mextractors call `[0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, which by default [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mallows external entity resolution. The secure pattern in POI is to use [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, which disables DTDs and external entities, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthereby mitigating SSRF.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Key Principles to Preserve  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Do not alter fuzzer harnesses, tests, or external dependencies.  [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Preserve existing extractor logic and exception signatures—only harden XML [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing.  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Reapply the prior intent to import `EXTENDED_PROPERTIES` and `XMLHelper` in [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe binary [0m[1;39m([0m[39m.xlsb[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m extractor, while restoring the `IOException` import.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Mirror the secure parsing pattern already used in [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.processSheet[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Steps  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. XSSFBEventBasedExcelExtractor.java [0m[1;39m([0m[39mbinary format extractor[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. **Restore the IOException import** at the top of the file.  [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Ensure the two previously added imports remain:[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - `import static [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39morg.apache.poi.openxml4j.opc.PackageRelationshipTypes.EXTENDED_PROPERTIES;`  [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        - `import org.apache.poi.util.XMLHelper;`  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Locate the `[0m[1;35mgetExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[39mStringBuilder text[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method. Replace the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minsecure parser instantiation:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m before[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        SAXParser parser = [0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m after[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        SAXParser parser = [0m[1;35mXMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Leave the catch block unchanged [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstill catching [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ParserConfigurationException | SAXException | IOException`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. XSSFEventBasedExcelExtractor.java [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOOXML .xlsx extractor[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Confirm it already imports `org.apache.poi.util.XMLHelper`. If not, add [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis import alongside the existing ones.  [0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Locate its `[0m[1;35mgetExtendedProps[0m[1;39m([0m[39mStringBuilder text[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m308[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mChange:[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```java[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m before[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        SAXParser parser = [0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m after[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        SAXParser parser = [0m[1;35mXMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        ```[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Ensure `import static [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39morg.apache.poi.openxml4j.opc.PackageRelationshipTypes.EXTENDED_PROPERTIES;` is [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpresent [0m[1;39m([0m[39mit may already be so, since the method uses the static constant[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. No changes to exception signatures or catch blocks.[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Restoring `IOException`** fixes the build errors without side effects or [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39maltering core functionality.  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Switching to `[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`** aligns with existing secure[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsing patterns [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., in `processSheet`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, fully neutralizing SSRF by disabling [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal entities and DTDs.  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - This approach only touches the two extractor classes, avoiding any test or [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mharness modifications, and preserves all existing extractor behaviors.  [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Side Effects & Mitigations  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - There is a theoretical risk that extremely exotic extended properties XML [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequiring external DTDs or schemas may now fail to parse. However, POI has [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mhistorically preferred robustness and security over external DTD resolution. Any [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregressions in XLSB or XLSX extended-properties extraction would manifest during [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnormal POI test runs. If needed, document this change in release notes.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Summary  [0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Re-add the missing `java.io.IOException` import in [0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`XSSFBEventBasedExcelExtractor.java`.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In both `.xlsx` and `.xlsb` event-based extractors, replace [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` with the securely configured [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXMLHelper.getSaxParserFactory[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Keep all other logic and exception handling intact to maintain backward [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcompatibility and satisfy existing tests.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJustification:[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Restores the missing `POIXMLDocument` symbol by re-importing and providing a [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconcrete implementation.[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Satisfies interface contract without deep API changes.[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Preserves event-based extraction performance and secure parser configuration.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Minimal side effects: `[0m[1;35mgetAllEmbeddedParts[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` uses existing package parts; [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39membedded parts usage is rare for text extraction.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
